## <a name="adam-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="16477-717">ADAM 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="16477-717">ADAM Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="16477-718">此類別包含 ADAM 的下列屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="16477-718">This class contains the following attributes for ADAM:</span></span>
